                    // this is a global that's called at the bottom of the pf.io response,

<script>
                    // Set the browserId from the bwid cookie on the ophan object created above
                    // This will need to be replaced later with an async request to an endpoint
                    (function (window, document) {

                        function getCookieValue(name) {
                            var nameEq = name + "=",
                                cookies = document.cookie.split(';'),
                                value = null;
                            cookies.forEach(function (cookie) {
                                while (cookie.charAt(0) === ' ') {
                                    cookie = cookie.substring(1, cookie.length);
                                }
                                if (cookie.indexOf(nameEq) === 0) {
                                    value = cookie.substring(nameEq.length, cookie.length);
                                }
                            });
                            return value;
                        }

                        window.guardian.config.ophan.browserId = getCookieValue("bwid");

                    })(window, document);
                </script>

		vertical-align: baseline;

		display: none;

		line-height: 1;

		list-style: none;
	}

		quotes: none;
	}

	q:before, q:after {
		content: '';
		content: none;
	}

		border-collapse: collapse;
		border-spacing: 0;
	}

class="dcr-5k6jfi" style="background-color:var(--masthead-nav-background);color:var(--masthead-nav-link-text)"><script>document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

					/** The checkbox input element used to toggle the navigation menu. */
					const navInputCheckbox = document.getElementById('header-nav-input-checkbox');

					/** The veggie burger button element used to open/close the menu. */
					const veggieBurger = document.getElementById('header-veggie-burger');

					/** List of menu items that should be selectable when the menu is open. */
					const expandedMenuClickableTags = document.querySelectorAll(
						'.selectableMenuItem',
					);

					/** The root element of the expanded menu. */
					const expandedMenu = document.getElementById('header-expanded-menu-root');

					/** The label for the first column in the menu, assumed to be "News".*/
					const firstColLabel = document.getElementById('News-button');

					/** The link element in the second list item under news links. */
					const firstColLink = document.querySelector(
						'#newsLinks > li:nth-of-type(2) > a',
					);

					/**
					 * Focuses on the first navigation element depending on whether the first column label is visible.
					 *
					 * If the first column label is not visible, the function focuses on the first link element.
					 * Otherwise, it focuses on the first column label.
					 */
					const focusOnFirstNavElement = () => {
						if (window.getComputedStyle(firstColLabel).display === 'none') {
							firstColLink.focus();
						} else {
							firstColLabel.focus();
						}
					};

					/**
					 * Updates ARIA attributes and tabindex values based on whether the menu is open or closed.
					 */
					const updateAttributesForMenu = (isOpen) => {
						firstColLabel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');
						veggieBurger.setAttribute(
							'data-link-name',
							isOpen
								? 'header : veggie-burger : hide'
								: 'header : veggie-burger : show',
						);
						expandedMenuClickableTags.forEach((tag) => {
							tag.setAttribute('tabindex', isOpen ? '0' : '-1');
						});
					};

					/** Toggles the navigation menu by simulating a click on the checkbox. */
					const toggleMainMenu = () => {
						if (navInputCheckbox) {
							navInputCheckbox.click();
						}
					};

					/**
					 * Handles keydown events to toggle the menu when the Enter or Space key is pressed.
					 */
					const keydownToggleMainMenu = (e) => {
						if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
							e.preventDefault();
							toggleMainMenu();
						}
					};
					/**
					 * Handles click events to manage the state of the navigation menu.
					 *
					 * - Toggles the menu open/close state when the menu button (veggieBurger) is clicked.
					 */
						const handleMenuClick = (e) => {
							const menuButtonClicked = navInputCheckbox === e.target;
							const clickInsideMenu = expandedMenu.contains(e.target);
							const menuIsOpen = navInputCheckbox.checked
							if (menuButtonClicked && !menuIsOpen) {
						    document.body.classList.toggle('nav-is-open')

							firstColLabel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false')
                            veggieBurger.setAttribute('data-link-name','header : veggie-burger : show')
                            expandedMenuClickableTags.forEach(function($selectableElement){
                                $selectableElement.setAttribute('tabindex','-1')
                            })
                          } else if (menuButtonClicked && menuIsOpen) {
						    document.body.classList.toggle('nav-is-open')
							firstColLabel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true')
                            veggieBurger.setAttribute('data-link-name','header : veggie-burger : hide')
                            expandedMenuClickableTags.forEach(function($selectableElement){
                                $selectableElement.setAttribute('tabindex','0')
                            })
                            focusOnFirstNavElement()
							}
						};

					/** Adds event listeners to manage the navigation menu. */
					if (navInputCheckbox) {
						navInputCheckbox.addEventListener('click', handleMenuClick);
						veggieBurger.addEventListener('keydown', keydownToggleMainMenu);
						document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
							if (e.key === 'Escape' && navInputCheckbox.checked) {
								toggleMainMenu();
								veggieBurger.focus();
							}
						});
					/**
					 * Handles mouse down events to manage the state of the navigation menu.
					 *
					 * - Closes the menu if the click occurs outside both the menu button and the expanded menu.
					 */
					document.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e){
						if(navInputCheckbox.checked && !expandedMenu.contains(e.target) && !veggieBurger.contains(e.target)){
						toggleMainMenu()
							}
						});
					}
				});</script><div class="dcr-1nph362"><div class="dcr-1mg0jui"><div class="dcr-1kbi9ft"><label class="dcr-8qc6v8" for="checkbox-id-masthead-edition">US</label><input aria-checked="false" <div data-did-prerender="true" id="gv-atom-contact-the-guardian"><div class="atom svelte-35jhdg"><div class="content svelte-35jhdg"><div class="header svelte-fezkfk" data-svelte-h="svelte-xphq8b"><h1 class="svelte-fezkfk">How to contact the Guardian securely</h1> <div class="big-phone svelte-fezkfk"><picture class="svelte-fezkfk"><source media="(max-width: 739px)" srcset="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/06/03/phone-small-screens.png"/> <img alt="" class="svelte-fezkfk" src="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/06/03/phone-light-large-screens.png"/></picture></div> <div class="page-preamble svelte-fezkfk"><p>Some of the most important stories published by the Guardian have come
			from confidential tips. If you have something sensitive to
			share with us, here’s how to get in touch.</p></div> </div> <div class="confidential-wrapper border-top svelte-35jhdg" data-svelte-h="svelte-13eglw3"><div class="confidential-and-anonymous svelte-35jhdg"><h3 class="svelte-35jhdg" id="confidential-and-anonymous">Confidential tips</h3> <p class="svelte-35jhdg">Journalists work closely with readers like you to investigate stories
					in the public interest. While no communication system is foolproof we
					go to great lengths to protect your identity and information. If
					you’re ready to share information with a journalist you’re in the
					right place, and we will treat you as a confidential journalistic
					source.</p> <p class="svelte-35jhdg">We rely on people sharing tips in the public interest – and we’re
					grateful that you’re thinking about getting in touch.</p></div> <img alt="" class="lamp svelte-35jhdg" src="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/06/03/lamp-light_opt.png"/></div> <div data-svelte-h="svelte-tgsswe"><h3 class="svelte-35jhdg">Composing your message</h3> <p class="svelte-35jhdg">We’re unlikely to pursue a lead unless we think it may lead to a news
					story, and we can't act on information that is vague or speculative.
					Our job is to hold power to account, to reveal institutional or
					systemic failings and to report on topics that are genuinely
					newsworthy. Please be clear, detailed and specific about your tip, why
					you think it matters, and what evidence you have.</p></div> <div class="crafting-your-message svelte-16jula5" data-svelte-h="svelte-9myler"><p class="svelte-16jula5"><span class="strong svelte-16jula5">Facts:</span> Specifics are critical, such as names,
		locations and dates.</p> <p class="dark-background svelte-16jula5">I work at <span class="yellow svelte-16jula5">government department ‘Department name’ in 
		the procurement section</span>.</p> <p class="svelte-16jula5"><span class="strong svelte-16jula5">Clearly state the nature of your tip:</span> Be concise 
		and focus on what you know, rather than what you think or suspect.</p> <p class="dark-background svelte-16jula5">I have discovered <span class="yellow svelte-16jula5">evidence of a senior official's 
		involvement in corruption and bribery</span>. ‘Name’, the head of our 
		section, has received $150,000 in under-the-radar payments.</p> <p class="svelte-16jula5"><span class="strong svelte-16jula5">Evidence:</span> Tell us how you know what you know,
		and how we might verify it.</p> <p class="dark-background last svelte-16jula5">I have <span class="yellow svelte-16jula5">photographic evidence of transactions</span> 
		from the past two years and access to <span class="yellow svelte-16jula5">further 
		documents</span> that show these were a quid pro quo for awarding 
		contracts to multinational company ‘Company name’.</p> </div> <section class="border-top svelte-35jhdg"><h3 class="svelte-35jhdg" data-svelte-h="svelte-1a4avdt">Choose your contact method</h3> <p class="svelte-35jhdg" data-svelte-h="svelte-p7vf24">There are many ways to contact the Guardian securely. Review the
				following options to see which one is best for you.</p> <div class="container svelte-1ozmpfo"><img alt="" class="floating-phone-one svelte-1ozmpfo" src="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/06/03/floating-phone-1_opt.png"/> <img alt="" class="floating-phone-two svelte-1ozmpfo" src="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/06/03/floating-phone-2_opt.png"/> <div class="card svelte-1ozmpfo"><svg fill="none" height="52" viewbox="0 0 52 52" width="52" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path clip-rule="evenodd" d="M16.7986 15.0745C16.7986 9.98246 20.9265 5.85458 26.0185 5.85458C31.1105 5.85458 35.2383 9.98246 35.2383 15.0745H38.9263C38.9263 7.94566 33.1473 2.16663 26.0185 2.16663C18.8897 2.16663 13.1106 7.94566 13.1106 15.0745H16.7986ZM13.1106 15.0745L13.1106 19.6844L11.2666 21.5284V43.656L13.1106 45.5H38.9262L40.7701 43.656V21.5284L38.9262 19.6845V15.0745H35.2383V19.6844H16.7985V15.0745H13.1106ZM28.7843 29.8263C28.7843 31.0306 28.0146 32.0551 26.9404 32.4348V36.2802H25.0964V32.4349C24.0221 32.0552 23.2524 31.0306 23.2524 29.8263C23.2524 28.2987 24.4907 27.0603 26.0183 27.0603C27.5459 27.0603 28.7843 28.2987 28.7843 29.8263Z" fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg> <h4 class="svelte-1ozmpfo" data-svelte-h="svelte-dfmr9j">SecureMessaging</h4> <p class="svelte-1ozmpfo" data-svelte-h="svelte-looq6e">Share your story with a journalist.
			<br/>
			Securely &amp; easily. Inside our news app.</p> <div data-svelte-h="svelte-cqr0ld"><span class="strong svelte-1ozmpfo">Pros:</span></div> <ul class="svelte-1ozmpfo" data-svelte-h="svelte-v9u9ae"><li class="svelte-1ozmpfo">Free and easy to download.</li> <li class="svelte-1ozmpfo">End-to-end encrypted.</li> <li class="svelte-1ozmpfo">Sending messages is indistinguishable from normal use of the Guardian app.</li> <li class="svelte-1ozmpfo">Connects you, anonymously if you choose, directly to our journalists.</li> <li class="svelte-1ozmpfo">Designed to be easy for everyone to use, without expert tech knowledge.</li></ul> <div data-svelte-h="svelte-fhag4w"><span class="strong svelte-1ozmpfo">Consider other platforms:</span></div> <ul class="svelte-1ozmpfo" data-svelte-h="svelte-noofaj"><li class="svelte-1ozmpfo">If you live or work in a place where the Guardian app is not safe to
				have on your device, scroll down for alternative ways to contact us.</li></ul></div> </div> <div class="wrapper svelte-kkx2pp"><div class="carousel svelte-kkx2pp"><div class="card svelte-14gb3x2"><div class="card-contents svelte-14gb3x2"><div class="details svelte-14gb3x2"><div class="step-name svelte-14gb3x2">Download the Guardian app</div> <div class="step-number svelte-14gb3x2">1 of 3</div></div> <img alt="Screenshot of the Guardian app in the app store" class="svelte-14gb3x2" src="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/06/03/1.get_the_app_opt.png"/></div> </div><div class="card svelte-14gb3x2"><div class="card-contents svelte-14gb3x2"><div class="details svelte-14gb3x2"><div class="step-name svelte-14gb3x2">Go to 'Secure Messaging' in the menu</div> <div class="step-number svelte-14gb3x2">2 of 3</div></div> <img alt="Screenshot of the Guardian app with the secure messaging option highlighted" class="svelte-14gb3x2" src="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/06/03/2.select_secure_messaging_opt.png"/></div> </div><div class="card svelte-14gb3x2"><div class="card-contents svelte-14gb3x2"><div class="details svelte-14gb3x2"><div class="step-name svelte-14gb3x2">Follow the instructions onscreen</div> <div class="step-number svelte-14gb3x2">3 of 3</div></div> <img alt="Screenshot of the Guardian app with the secure messaging start page" class="svelte-14gb3x2" src="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/06/03/3.secure_messaging_startpage_opt.png"/></div> </div></div> </div> <div class="badge-container svelte-9kh529" data-svelte-h="svelte-1r7815h"><div class="store-link svelte-9kh529"><a href="https://apps.apple.com/app/the-guardian-live-world-news/id409128287" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><img alt="Download on the App Store" class="svelte-9kh529" src="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/04/23/apple-app-store-badge.png"/></a></div> <div class="store-link svelte-9kh529"><a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.guardian" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><img alt="Get it on Google Play" class="svelte-9kh529" src="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/02/11/google-play-badge.png"/></a></div> </div> <div class="option-card option-0 svelte-bj4ffe"><div class="icon svelte-bj4ffe"><svg class="svelte-j3usbx" fill="none" height="52" viewbox="0 0 52 52" width="52" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink"><rect fill="url(#pattern0_695_5593)" height="52" width="44" x="4"></rect><defs><pattern height="1" id="pattern0_695_5593" patterncontentunits="objectBoundingBox" width="1"><use transform="matrix(0.0051161 0 0 0.004329 -0.0116096 0)" xlink:href="#securedrop-icon-light-mode"></use><use transform="matrix(0.0051161 0 0 0.004329 -0.0116096 0)" xlink:href="#securedrop-icon-dark-mode"></use></pattern><image class="light svelte-j3usbx" height="231" href="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/02/11/securedrop-icon-light-mode.png" id="securedrop-icon-light-mode" width="200"/><image class="dark svelte-j3usbx" height="231" href="https://uploads.guim.co.uk/2025/02/11/securedrop-icon-dark-mode.png" id="securedrop-icon-dark-mode" width="200"/></defs></svg></div> <h4 class="svelte-bj4ffe">SecureDrop</h4> <div class="content"><p class="description svelte-bj4ffe">Our SecureDrop system is a great way to contact us and to send documents. However, it does require more technical preparation.</p> <div class="expandable hide svelte-bj4ffe"><h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-160xny4">Pros:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-q6hhhi"><li>SecureDrop does not record where things come from.</li> <li>All material is encrypted automatically.</li> <li>We read your submissions on secure computers.</li></ul> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1lvl2pt">Cons:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-z0dvi7"><li>You will need to download Tor software to access our SecureDrop system.</li> <li>If you are being watched, the very act of using Tor may arouse suspicion.</li></ul> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1r93a8k">SecureDrop allows you to safely send us messages and documents, and to follow
	up with us later if you wish. All we get is what you send us plus a codename
	that allows us to reply to you. SecureDrop records nothing else about you. To
	prevent interception at our end, we decrypt any material that you send us on 
	a system that is completely offline.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-u3erdl">Get started:</h5> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-v6d3tn">On a computer that you are confident is not being monitored, install <a href="https://www.torproject.org/download/">Tor Browser</a>. Then go to theguardian.com/securedrop and follow the instructions there.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1ku9fmn">After that:</h5> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-s2ppof">When you first visit our SecureDrop site itself, you will be given a 
	passphrase before you can send anything. This phrase allows you to log back in 
	to view replies from us and to continue correspondence, if you so wish. 
	We do not always reply to messages and even when we do, responses can take several days.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-176or1l">SecureDrop is quite a slow way to communicate, so after you have begun
	corresponding with a reporter they may suggest a more direct way to interact.
	You don’t have to agree to this, of course, but it can make things smoother
	under some circumstances.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-10pibz0">SecureDrop is an open source project managed by the <a href="https://freedom.press/">Freedom of the Press Foundation</a>.</p> </div></div> <div class="link svelte-bj4ffe" role="button" tabindex="0">Show more <div class="chevron svelte-bj4ffe"><svg fill="none" height="24" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path clip-rule="evenodd" d="M1 7.22436L11.4977 17.7221H12.5023L23 7.22436L22.0205 6.27002L12 14.7084L1.97945 6.27002L1 7.22436Z" fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div> </div><div class="option-card option-1 svelte-bj4ffe"><div class="icon svelte-bj4ffe"><svg fill="none" height="38" viewbox="0 0 40 38" width="40" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path clip-rule="evenodd" d="M39.4999 4.08324L36.2499 0.833252H3.74999L0.5 4.08324V23.5832L3.69582 26.8332H9.16664V37.6665H11.2791L17.8333 26.8332H36.2499L39.4999 23.5832V4.08324Z" fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div> <h4 class="svelte-bj4ffe">Instant messenger apps</h4> <div class="content"><p class="description svelte-bj4ffe">End to end encrypted messaging apps such as Signal and WhatsApp provide good protection for the content of your messages, and are very easy to use.</p> <div class="expandable hide svelte-bj4ffe"> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1hawcoo">Signal is trusted by journalists, human rights activists and security experts
	worldwide, and is our recommended instant messaging app. WhatsApp, while not 
	quite as secure, also encrypts the content of communications and benefits from 
	being so ubiquitous that using it is unlikely (in itself) to raise suspicion 
	in most parts of the world. Other secure messenger apps tend to be less widely 
	used for communication between sources and our journalists.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-160xny4">Pros:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-1bcv6el"><li>They’re very easy to use.</li> <li>They allow for speedy back-and-forth communication.</li> <li>Everything is encrypted in transit and on the service providers’ servers, so
		not even they can read the content of your messages.</li></ul> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1lvl2pt">Cons:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-7unkax"><li>On WhatsApp, information about the participants in a conversation is less
		secure than the content itself.</li> <li>There are ways for very sophisticated adversaries, such as government spy 
		agencies, to ascertain that someone is communicating with a journalist 
		using messaging apps – even if they can’t read the message content.</li> <li>Instant messenger communication requires advance knowledge of the
		participants’ contact details. For WhatsApp it must be a phone number; for
		Signal it can be a username or phone number. Many journalists are reluctant
		to publish their personal contact details widely because such information 
		can be abused.</li></ul> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1aoersl">It’s not uncommon for conversations with journalists to shift to instant messenger
	apps once both sides have established some trust and have discussed the
	benefits and risks. But you or the journalist may decide not to use them.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-u3erdl">Get started:</h5> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1l4olyd">Decide whether you want to do this on your normal phone or if you want to buy
	a less easily traceable phone for this purpose. After installing the app, make
	it as secure as possible: if there are extra authentication options, activate
	them. And activate disappearing messages so your conversations don’t sit
	around forever on your device.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-124vroo">Read more about Signal <a href="https://signal.org/">here</a> 
	and about WhatsApp <a href="https://www.whatsapp.com/privacy">here</a>.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1ku9fmn">After that:</h5> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1csfyry">If you’re worried about surveillance and you’ve not used the app before,
	consider using it for few innocuous purposes first, such as exchanging 
	messages with friends. That way, when you message us, your use of the app 
	doesn’t look out of the ordinary.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-16xtt1p">Signal/WhatsApp numbers for our investigations teams:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-16q465u"><li>United Kingdom: +44 7721 857348</li> <li>United States: +1 646 886 8761</li> <li>Australia: +61 490 758 250</li></ul> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-e4eqrz">Please don’t call or send ordinary text messages to those numbers. You won’t
	get a reply.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-bz1jyw">Check our journalists’ profile pages for other contact details.
	Google their name and “the Guardian” and you should find them. If you can’t
	find the right contact details for the journalist, you could message one of
	the above numbers and ask for your details to be passed on to the person you
	have in mind.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1hbjz3b">Please note the recommendations earlier in this guide for what to say about 
	the information you wish to share.</p> </div></div> <div class="link svelte-bj4ffe" role="button" tabindex="0">Show more <div class="chevron svelte-bj4ffe"><svg fill="none" height="24" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path clip-rule="evenodd" d="M1 7.22436L11.4977 17.7221H12.5023L23 7.22436L22.0205 6.27002L12 14.7084L1.97945 6.27002L1 7.22436Z" fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div> </div><div class="option-card option-2 svelte-bj4ffe"><div class="icon svelte-bj4ffe"><svg height="52" viewbox="0 0 52 52" width="52" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M5.57151 8.66675L2.16675 12.3469L23.7302 29.5209H28.2699L49.8334 12.3469L46.4287 8.66675H5.57151Z" fill="currentColor"></path><path d="M2.16675 38.1876V17.6042L23.7302 32.7709H28.2699L49.8334 17.6042V38.1876L46.4287 41.4376H5.57151L2.16675 38.1876Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></div> <h4 class="svelte-bj4ffe">Email</h4> <div class="content"><p class="description svelte-bj4ffe">Use a tailor-made email account to make it less obvious that you are in contact with a journalist.</p> <div class="expandable hide svelte-bj4ffe"> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-12hmrn0">If the information you wish to share with us isn’t extremely sensitive, 
	email is probably the easiest way to get in touch. Even so, you may 
	consider it worthwhile to put a bit of distance between your messages 
	to a journalist and the rest of your life. Plus, because journalists 
	receive so many emails, you should take extra care to make sure your 
	message doesn’t get lost in the noise.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-160xny4">Pros:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-pealtq"><li>Everyone knows how to use email, and many Guardian journalists publish
		their email addresses.</li> <li>You can send long messages and attachments. This is difficult using phone
		apps.</li> <li>It's possible (but not straightforward) to add encryption to email messages.</li></ul> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1lvl2pt">Cons:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-wb6pvz"><li>Normal emails are not at all secure. Your correspondence can be monitored. 
		Even a purpose-built email account can reveal information about you.</li> <li>Adding encryption to emails is difficult and does not hide some information
		(who is talking to whom, the subject lines, etc).</li></ul> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-q12b28">Email is an inherently insecure medium but you can do some things to make your 
	correspondence less likely to be intercepted.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-u3erdl">Get started:</h5> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1q8yoet">Don’t use your regular work or personal email address. Create a new email account 
	solely for corresponding with the Guardian. Do this on a computer that can't easily
	be linked back to you.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-2ld7le">When you sign up for a new email account, make sure the sign-up information 
	you provide doesn’t tie the account back to you. Never use the same password 
	for different accounts.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1ku9fmn">After that:</h5> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1ld4foe">Because it's so easy to send emails, journalists often receive a lot of spurious
	and irrelevant messages. So anything that doesn't get their attention quickly may 
	be overlooked. Read the advice further up in this guide about what makes a 
	good story tip.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1ckexrm">Information carried with an email message can reveal your IP address. 
	If you don’t want the location you send from to be traceable, connect to your 
	email service over the Tor network. or send from somewhere that doesn’t easily identify you.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-sr1bew">Remember to log out after sending the message. You may also wish to delete the 
	history of the correspondence from your browser or email software. Keep your computer secure.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1ufe8zd">Some Guardian journalists publish PGP keys, allowing you to encrypt the content
	of email messages (but not the subject line or the fact that you are communicating with them).
	See theguardian.com/pgp.</p> </div></div> <div class="link svelte-bj4ffe" role="button" tabindex="0">Show more <div class="chevron svelte-bj4ffe"><svg fill="none" height="24" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path clip-rule="evenodd" d="M1 7.22436L11.4977 17.7221H12.5023L23 7.22436L22.0205 6.27002L12 14.7084L1.97945 6.27002L1 7.22436Z" fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div> </div><div class="option-card option-3 svelte-bj4ffe"><div class="icon svelte-bj4ffe"><svg fill="none" height="52" viewbox="0 0 52 52" width="52" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path clip-rule="evenodd" d="M35.7236 2.16675L39 5.44317V46.557L35.7236 49.7806L16.2764 49.8334L13 46.557V5.44317L16.2764 2.16675H35.7236ZM26.2114 46.557C27.374 46.557 28.3781 45.6058 28.3781 44.3904C28.3781 43.1749 27.374 42.2237 26.2114 42.2237C24.996 42.2237 23.9919 43.1749 23.9919 44.3904C23.9919 45.6058 24.996 46.557 26.2114 46.557ZM34.8252 40.057V9.72365H17.4919V40.057H34.8252Z" fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div> <h4 class="svelte-bj4ffe">Telephone</h4> <div class="content"><p class="description svelte-bj4ffe">Although telephone communication is far from secure, it can be a practical way to get a conversation started.</p> <div class="expandable hide svelte-bj4ffe"> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-160xny4">Pros:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-yl038b"><li>Requires no technical prowess.</li> <li>Useful to initiate communication with a journalist to exchange contact
		information for more secure channels.</li></ul> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1lvl2pt">Cons:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-1xubrk5"><li>Telephone communication can be intercepted and could reveal your identity
		and/or location.</li> <li>It’s not always easy to verify that the person you’re speaking to is who
		they say they are.</li></ul> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-u3erdl">Get started:</h5> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1wgnlpj">Before you get in touch, find the name of the journalist you want to speak to,
	and decide in advance exactly how much you want to tell them about who you are
	and how they can get back to you. The journalist you want may not be available
	when you call, so you may have to leave a message. Be prepared for that.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1ka24x">If you plan to share documents with us later, look at some of the other
	options in this guide before calling so you can tell the journalist how you’d
	prefer to do that.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-en9i3v">Consider whether or not it is safe to call us from your work or home phone, or
	from any mobile phone that is associated with you. If you buy a pay-as-you-go
	sim card to call us from a new number, think carefully about where and when
	you buy it, and how you pay for it. And remember that mobile phone calls
	disclose the handset ID as well as the sim card.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1ku9fmn">After that:</h5> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1bv4299">Call us on one of these numbers:</p> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-al0r90"><li>London office: +44 (0)20 3353 2000</li> <li>Sydney office: +61 (0)2 8076 8500</li> <li>New York office: +1 212 231 7762</li> <li>Washington office: +1 202 517 89042</li> <li>San Francisco office: +1 415 919 5874</li></ul> </div></div> <div class="link svelte-bj4ffe" role="button" tabindex="0">Find the number you need <div class="chevron svelte-bj4ffe"><svg fill="none" height="24" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path clip-rule="evenodd" d="M1 7.22436L11.4977 17.7221H12.5023L23 7.22436L22.0205 6.27002L12 14.7084L1.97945 6.27002L1 7.22436Z" fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div> </div><div class="option-card option-4 svelte-bj4ffe"><div class="icon svelte-bj4ffe"><svg fill="currentColor" height="52" viewbox="0 0 200 200" width="52" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M146 60.25C168.091 60.25 186 78.1586 186 100.25V167.75H117.2V93.7998C117.2 79.7443 109.949 67.3838 98.9854 60.25H146Z"></path><path d="M60 60.25C82.0914 60.25 100 78.1586 100 100.25V167.75H14V100.25C14 78.1586 31.9086 60.25 54 60.25H60ZM35.5 114V124.75H78.5V114H35.5Z"></path><path d="M169 22V32L161 40H136V64H122V14H161L169 22Z"></path></svg></div> <h4 class="svelte-bj4ffe">Postal mail</h4> <div class="content"><p class="description svelte-bj4ffe">Post still has its uses, especially if you want to send us hard copies.</p> <div class="expandable hide svelte-bj4ffe"> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-160xny4">Pros:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-dn4m49"><li>If appropriate measures are taken, conventional mail can be a reasonably
		good way to hide who you are.</li> <li>If you don’t want to meet a journalist in person, it’s the only reliable way
		to hand over physical objects.</li></ul> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1lvl2pt">Cons:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-lip3qa"><li>It’s slow.</li> <li>Post can get hijacked or at least scanned in transit.</li> <li>Post can get lost.</li></ul> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-198qwr">If you’re not actually being followed it’s fairly unlikely that an envelope or
	small package will get intercepted.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-u3erdl">Get started:</h5> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-1aiiouv">Stuff can go missing in the post, so consider how bad it would be to lose the
	material you’re planning to send us. Can you make copies?</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-394kjz">Think about whether or not you need to preserve your anonymity. Could the
	posting location give you up? How about the materials and packaging? If you’re
	very worried about the package being traced back to you, post it somewhere
	busy and make sure there is nothing memorable about your or the package’s
	appearance.</p> <p data-svelte-h="svelte-4xo4ns">Mail is scanned for dangerous compounds and objects. Don’t include anything
	that could cause problems with delivery. International mail needs a customs
	declaration, and registered mail requires you to provide sender details.</p> <h5 data-svelte-h="svelte-1ku9fmn">After that:</h5> <ul data-svelte-h="svelte-74of12"><li>Guardian UK postal address:
		<br/>
		The Guardian
		<br/>
		Kings Place
		<br/>
		90 York Way
		<br/>
		London N1 9GU
		<br/>
		United Kingdom</li> <li>Guardian US postal address:
		<br/>
